Free Talk

World Anecdotes 171

— Sea Guest

The Story of Beards

In ancient Eastern nations, there was a deep-rooted superstition that a man's beard was a symbol of honor, and to punish someone, they would forcibly shave off their beard and cut their hair short. However, looking at ancient Assyrian sculptures, the images of the emperors all have long beards flowing down their chests. Their hair is also always long, while the slaves serving them have no beards at all, their faces are clean-shaven, and their hair is cut extremely short. The difference between the noble and the lowly is, of course, immediately apparent.

The Egyptians, however, had different opinions from the Assyrians. They believed that beards and hair were filthy things and that the head and face must be completely shaved. Their slaves and servants were also forced to do the same and were not allowed to grow them long.

Ancient Greeks and Romans often suffered greatly when fighting with enemies because their beards were grabbed. Therefore, they all shaved off their beards. It is said that King Alexander the Great strictly ordered his soldiers to shave their beards for this reason.

In ancient Roman customs, men at the age of twenty-one had to shave off their beards and offer them to the statues of the gods in their homes. Growing a beard after this age was only done when a family member died.

Funny Stories at the Road Exhibition 172

— Sun Choucheng

The China National Road Construction Association has been established for ten years. The Road City Exhibition will be held for three weeks starting on September 12 this year. The other day, Chairman Wang Zhengting specially invited Chinese and Western people to discuss the methods of implementation. Many funny stories were told at the meeting. I will record one or two of them below.

Wang Zhengting's Eyes Don't Close Wang Zhengting said that roads are to the country as blood vessels are to the human body. If the blood vessels don't circulate, the person will surely die. If the roads are not developed, the country will be difficult to strengthen. When I was in Peiping (Beijing) before, I met a Western friend who mentioned the inconvenience of transportation in our country. He had a few words that I will never forget. He said, for example, if someone in Tibet sent me two bags of flour and wanted me to take them back to Peiping, I would rather telegraph from Peiping to Washington, D.C. to order two bags of flour. Because transportation from Tibet to Peiping is inconvenient, these two bags of flour must be carried by camels and transported by small carts along the way. Although the goods are given as a gift, the transportation costs are actually more valuable than the flour purchased in the United States. Although it is a joke, it is indeed the truth. Therefore, when I initiated the National Road Construction Association, I had a wish to assist the government and local areas in building roads in all provinces across the country, and then ride in a car and travel around all provinces of China for a week. If I can achieve this goal, I will have no regrets even in death. Since the promotion of this association, about 110,000 li of roads have been completed. However, our country is vast, and it is still a long way to go to travel around by car. If this goal is not achieved, my eyes will not close after death. I hope you all will vigorously promote the road construction movement, etc. The listeners were amused.

Lin Kanghou Fears Heatstroke Wu Shan, the executive director of the association, reported in public that a total of 100,000 entrance tickets were printed for the Road City Exhibition this time. Each ticket sells for one yuan to subsidize the expenses of the meeting. The tickets are sold by Chinese and Western people, each selling 50,000. Lin Kanghou is responsible for the Chinese side, for which we are very grateful. Wang Zhengting was very impressed by Lin's enthusiasm and insisted that he stand up and give advice. Lin said that the weather is hot today, and you are putting a high hat on my head, so I can't handle it and I'm afraid I'll get heatstroke. The reason why I joined this association and took on the position of director of the general affairs group is that things in our country have not been on the right track recently. If we want to get on the right track, we must first build roads. Therefore, I have contributed some opinions on the ticket sales. It is not that I am solely responsible for all 50,000 tickets. I still need to ask people from all walks of life to sell them on my behalf. I recently learned that Minister Wang and Zilian have each recognized 10,000 tickets, so my responsibility has been reduced by two-fifths. For the rest, please have the chairman come forward to invite people from all walks of life to the meeting to encourage them to purchase. I believe it will be easy to find a way.

Zhang Zhijiang Doesn't Forget His Roots The association invited Zhang Zhijiang to succeed Jiang Baiqi as vice chairman after Jiang Baiqi passed away. Zhang said that road construction has a great relationship with local security. For example, if bandits come to attack, it is easy to eliminate them if troops can be mobilized within one or two hours from a distance of hundreds of li. If roads are not built and transportation is inconvenient, if troops from a distance of hundreds of li must be gathered within one or two days, the bandits will unexpectedly loot and escape long ago, and there will be no way to pursue them. The area will be devastated. Everyone said that Zhang is currently the Superintendent of Jiangnan Pacification, and is handling bandit suppression affairs in Jiangbei. He doesn't leave his profession in three sentences, which shows his concern for his own duties.

Consoling Successful Judges 173

— Tao Zaidong

I remember a Ming Dynasty poem about the Hundred Horses Picture: "Ninety-nine of them are all sweating blood, the first one is the Longmei." This is a famous line. Ninety-nine people below Zhu Leizhang have been selected in this high-level examination. I secretly thought that Mr. Liu, who was wrongly divided, must be added to make up a hundred horses. Although I don't know who the Longmei belongs to, ninety-nine of them are strong horses. Therefore, the government's treatment is extremely generous. On the day of awarding the certificates, all the officials accompanied him. The ceremony was solemn and the instructions were added. The general gift is a silver commemorative badge, and the special award is a complete collection of the Prime Minister's books and a compilation of Building the Nation Monthly. President Shao Yuanchong and Ms. Zhang Mojun gave a mirror and inscribed a fan. These are unusual numbers. As for the ceremony of visiting the mausoleum, it is the same as releasing vegetables. The banquet at the shoes forest is no different from the Qionglin. It is also said that a memorial tablet is planned to be erected in front of the mausoleum, which is the legacy of the Tang Yan Pagoda and the Ming Taixue Jinshi inscriptions. The students also set up a reunion of the same year. It is said that a new item can be added to the party friendship, and the old friendship will not be abolished. In short, the country glorifies the success of the examination. Lucky are the ninety-nine people. However, there are still 150 people crying in the corner. Who are the 150 people? They are the judges who passed the first examination of the trial court last year. In this campaign, the recruitment began with the Judicial Yuan and ended with the Examination Yuan. The Legislative Yuan has a special case. Although the period is divided into two years, the examination is actually the same. Therefore, this year's five examinations are uniquely lacking in the judicial one because of this. The Examination Yuan awarded certificates to 150 people and consulted the Judicial Yuan to order the Ministry of Justice to establish a special office for training, retraining, internships, and more internships. It is limited to one and a half years as a reserve for promotion and inspection. In terms of results, it is almost better than the ninety-nine new entrants. However, the glory is not shared by them. How can we satisfy the youthful competitive spirit and show the country's importance to judicial candidates? The members of the office met me and seemed to be indignant. I first corrected them and said, "Scholars value practical learning and do not value empty words. Huan Rong of the Han Dynasty extravagantly displayed his carriages and clothes to show off his glory in studying the past. Wang Panshan read the Tongjianlun and despised him. This is why Han Weigong of the Song Dynasty refused to wear flowers after passing the examination and eventually became a famous Confucian and minister." I comforted them again and said, "Selecting talents and honors is to value the legacy of education and encourage morale. New visions and directions will be shown in the future. At the beginning of the founding of the country, the scale was new, and there was no time to spare. There may be omissions. There must be ways to pick up the omissions. How can there be six selections, five of which are grand and one of which is neglected? Do not be impatient, you two or three children."

Anecdotes from the Calamity 174

— Zou Jinshi

I, the unworthy one, have traveled between Shanghai and Hangzhou. Incessantly, I have experienced the changing seasons five times. This time, upon my mother's command, I took leave to return to my hometown. The communist scourge is rampant, and nine out of ten homes are empty. The once-renowned Zhejiang as a land of happiness, where can it be found now? What I have heard and seen, I will record a bit of it.

My county (Ruian) is thirty miles south across the Feiyun River, known as Pingyang. River steamers travel back and forth in half a day. Pingyang is indeed a land of scenic mountains and clear waters, with pure customs and abundant products, surpassing all in the Southeast. Last year, in May, the area was originally garrisoned by a company of provincial defense troops stationed in the City God Temple north of the city. The statues of the impermanent officials there were terrifying and hideous. The people of the county believed them to be extremely efficacious, offering incense and prayers abundantly. Since the troops were stationed there, the people of the county had not been allowed to enter the temple for several months. On the 26th of that month, before noon, the provincial defense troops received orders to move out. Many soldiers carried guns, ready to depart. Just then, the gun of a certain platoon leader of the troop was suddenly missing. They searched everywhere. After about two hours, it was finally found under the seat of the Impermanence God. By then, it was noon. They then started cooking in the temple. While they were having lunch, a report suddenly came that bandits were arriving. At that time, the guide for the bandits intended to lead them to disarm the troops here. Unexpectedly, they lost their way. The government troops then took the opportunity to climb the city walls together and shoot. Every shot hit its mark, with no wasted bullets. Hundreds of communist bandits were spared. During the battle between the troops and the bandits, the government troops, fearing they were outnumbered, sent a messenger to request reinforcements from my county. The messenger returned in just one hour. Even more strange, it rained heavily all night that day. The firewood, oil, and other flammable materials the bandits carried could not be ignited. Someone even poured oil on the firewood to set fire to a house, but the matches suddenly disappeared. When they came out of the house, they were still there. This happened again and again. The bandits were furious and just beat on the house. In this battle, hundreds of enemies were killed, while only one government soldier died. This can be considered fortunate.

The magistrate announced that Pingyang's transformation from danger to safety was due to several extraordinary occurrences. First, the army losing its gun and delaying the time, leading to the troops killing the enemy, was one extraordinary event. Second, the guide getting lost, preventing the disarmament, was the second extraordinary event. Next, the matches suddenly disappearing, preventing arson, was the third extraordinary event. Next, wiping out hundreds of enemies with only one soldier killed was the fourth extraordinary event. Because of these four extraordinary events, the people of Pingyang all said it was divine assistance.

Further Record of Zhu Yongkui's Engraving Skills 175

— Yan Chonglou

I once wrote for this newspaper about Mr. Zhu Yongkui's superb engraving skills, and those who heard of it marveled at it. However, there were still some things that were not fully explained, so I will record them again as follows.

Mr. Zhu can engrave three thousand characters on a piece of ivory the size of an inch. Therefore, it cannot be recognized by the naked eye. One must use a very precise microscope to find the vigorous, elegant, and neat characters. However, Mr. Zhu never uses the aid of a mirror when engraving. After more than ten years of research, he has entered a realm of mastery. What is even more amazing is that the knife Mr. Zhu uses to engrave characters is no different from the ones used for ordinary engraving. It is unknown how a large knife can engrave such tiny, ant-like characters.

I once saw him engrave an ivory ring for a certain gentleman. The ring face was engraved with "Oath of Love," about hundreds of words. It was intended to be a gift to his beloved, to be remembered forever. Other items, such as fan bones, cigarette holders, and ivory chopsticks, can also be engraved with characters on them, which is also very interesting.

In addition to being good at engraving ivory, Mr. Zhu is also good at engraving bamboo. His skills are also exquisite. I heard that he will use his engraving skills for fellow enthusiasts in his spare time from academic affairs. His friends have already set the price, two jiao per word. Those who love his art can go directly to the National Academy of Music to discuss with him in person.

Travel Notes of India (88) 176

— Linghua

On the eleventh, I was invited by the University of India to participate in the ceremony of building the VIWANATB Temple. Visuna means the master of the world. Almost all Indian names contain the idea of conquering the world. This is one of them. As for what god it is and what era it is from, it is not known. There was wind that day, and a lot of dust. A large cloth shed was set up on the open space of the university. More than 10,000 people arrived, including many women. Outside the venue was a wheat field, where wheat was being harvested. There were trees next to it, and many people climbed the trees to admire the scene of the meeting. I arrived late, and only saw that the chairman was a naked, bare-skinned man. This is truly a naked man here. It is different from what I have seen in various meetings. The naked men at various meetings still have an inch or so of cloth around them. This naked man showed the true body given by his parents, including his reproductive organs. He sat in the right position as chairman, wearing various flower garlands, and his hair was rolled into a bun like a Chinese Taoist. However, he is truly virtuous. Chinese Taoists are all fake people. This is a real person. His name is KRISH丨NASHRM. He is about forty years old, with a black beard of several inches, bright eyes, a fat body, and thick, black skin, probably because he has been assimilated with nature for a long time. Among the ten thousand people, his reproductive organs were also exposed. I saw it very clearly. This is probably the number one immortal in the world. Why does he need to be the number one immortal? The number one mountain in the world is the Himalayas. He went to this mountain for fourteen years. He never speaks. This time, he was specially invited by the University of India to preside over the opening ceremony of the temple. Therefore, he descended to this meeting. Soon, he will return to the cave of the number one mountain. The naked immortal sometimes got up and operated an iron chain. Everyone got up to watch. The master of ceremonies forbade them to stand up, but I don't know why. The person standing next to him was the speaker, named MAVIA. MOHANMALVIYA spoke using a radio. The entire audience could hear him. Unfortunately, I don't understand Indian. He said that this meeting was intended to seek peace for men and women all over the world. I went to this meeting too late. I only saw the naked real person, which can be called a wonder of the world. But I am not only curious, but I also know the strange. Buddhist and Taoist books all say that cultivators who become immortals cultivate into a concealed yin-horse phase. What is the concealed yin-horse phase? It means that a man's yang tool shrinks internally due to cultivation and is not exposed externally. The Infinite Meaning Sutra describes one of the Buddha's thirty-two phases as the concealed yin-horse phase, which means that the yang tool is not exposed externally. The first book says that women who cultivate cut off menstruation, which is called cutting off the red dragon. Now this number one immortal's yang tool is exposed externally. I don't know if his Tao has not yet been achieved, or if the cultivation methods are different. However, the Buddha used to sit quietly on Snow Mountain for six years and did not attain enlightenment. The Buddha himself said that he finally attained it through enlightenment. Cultivation is done on Snow Mountain, and enlightenment is attained on the plains of Gaya. Also, when the Buddha cultivated for six years, the old seniors at the time did not believe it, saying that he was a prince, unable to endure hardship, and too pampered. We have been cultivating hard for eight years and have not yet attained enlightenment. Now this immortal has been cultivating for fourteen years. I don't know if he has attained enlightenment or not. He doesn't say, so I don't know. But in the past, when Bodhidharma came to the East, he faced the wall for ten years without speaking. Bodhidharma testified to this. This immortal can not speak, so he is probably a type of Bodhidharma.

Lakeside Pavilion Poetry Talk (Part 1) 177

— Tianxu Wosheng

This time for the Lakeside Pavilion poetry lessons, unexpectedly many veterans of the poetry scene also came with great interest. How dare I presumptuously judge the merits of each entry. Moreover, there were more than six hundred volumes, with a dazzling array of impressive works. Unfortunately, I have no time to read them in detail. However, a cursory glance might disappoint people. Therefore, I first sent them to Cuiyin Pavilion to have them circle the acceptable lines. Then, I, the humble one, made a second selection and added circles. As a result, there is hardly anyone whose four poems are all excellent, with double circles for every line. Flaws and merits are interwoven, and even Li Bai and Du Fu could not avoid this. Since this is not a talent selection ceremony, why bother to interpret the order of names, which could provoke feelings of honor and disgrace. Therefore, I will extract lines for detailed commentary and choose the best to reveal as follows.

For the first line of the first poem, "After the vernal equinox, the days gradually lengthen" is the best. Because the winter solstice has the shortest days, and the summer solstice has the longest days, the vernal equinox is the midpoint from short to long, and the autumnal equinox is the midpoint from long to short. Therefore, this line with its three embedded characters actually contains scientific knowledge and is very reliable. Something like "After the new autumn, the days gradually cool" would be more general. The second-best is "The painting shoulder picks up the wave light in the low place." because the words "picks up" and "low" are quite evocative and create a coherent whole. Something like "connects with mountain light" or "presses against mountain light" - the word "presses" may be slightly better than "connects", but is not as fluid as "picks up". The third line, "The curtain waves seem to move as the breeze rises" is the best, using the word "seem" to echo the word "breeze", making every word feel outstanding. It is truly worthy of praise. The fourth line is "Lotus leaves fill the pond, the shadows of people are fragrant" is the best. However, these four lines were not all written by the same person. Therefore, the word "wave" is repeated. However, changing "wave light" to "lake light" or "fill the pond" to "fill the pool" would also diminish the beauty somewhat. The "wave" in "curtain wave" is related to the words "move" and "breeze" and "rises" and must not be changed. Now, this is poetry talk, not a poetry selection. Using analytical methods to consider the words and phrases is like cutting jade, discarding the flaws and taking the merits. It is not necessary to be like gathering armpits to make a fur coat, seeking a flaw in the hair.

For the first and second lines of the second poem, "The sound of insects comes through the window screen at night, the Milky Way is silent, and the moon is half-slanted" is more stable. Because the silence of the Milky Way sets off the sound of insects, and the half-slanting moon sets off the word "through". And taking "Deeper the night, the moonlight, half the people's homes" as a blueprint, you can feel the connection up and down, and it is a circle worth reciting. Other works are mostly superficial and inevitably have differences in skill. The third and fourth lines connect with "Who is rowing a small boat to seek the old agreement? Ask the Su family by the West Lake Bridge", which is the most appropriate. Because "rowing a small boat to seek the old agreement" is a complete song title, and Su Xiao of West Lake is already a dead person. Who still cares? It seems to be the sound of insects at night saying what the author hears. These fantasies are most appreciated by the poetry scene. This whole poem can be said to be seamless.

For the second and second lines of the third poem, "Peach blossoms bloom in the clear weather after the rain, listen to the oriole in the green willow shade" should be chosen. Using "peach blossom" to echo the words "bloom" and "tender", and using "green willow" to echo the word "shade" is extremely clever. Something like "crying oriole" would inevitably be dull, or "weeping willow" would not have the echoes of the words "green" and "shade". The third and fourth lines should take "A road for pedestrians around the lake, even Ni Zan and Huang Gongwang could not paint it." The last sentence is redundant. There are many who change one or two words. The upper sentence is not to create a gazetteer for the new West Lake, because all the lakeside areas and the water's edge have pedestrian paths. People walking on them, with reflections in the water, truly cannot be described by painting. The pedestrian path is a term in the architectural world. Being able to use colloquial language in poetry is not annoying and is truly the essence of the bamboo branch. The last sentence uses a reverse writing method, which is more similar to the upright behavior of Ni Zan and Huang Gongwang in painting.

The Yarn, Flower, and Yarn Markets Are Fluctuating 184

The trend of the yarn market is chaotic and inconsistent, and the market conditions are still brewing. It rises and falls suddenly, making it difficult to grasp. The distant months are hovering between 52 and 3 taels. In short, the world's cotton industry is deteriorating, so the big households unanimously sell. A certain giant merchant still enters the near and leaves the far. However, the raw materials for coarse yarn are cheaper, and the profit from spinning coarse yarn is still not bad, so there is no lack of short sellers. However, a certain manufacturer is tightening and still does not relax. However, the actual sales have been good recently, so the market conditions are tight one step. However, the environment is more severe. In the afternoon, the price of third-grade yarn rose by 34 yuan, and it is expected that American cotton has the power to rise, and the market plate is rising.

The afternoon market rose slightly, and the market opened in the previous market. As the price of American cotton rose slightly, the situation was relatively false, and each month fell by 1, 3, and 4 qian. The market opened in the afternoon, which was very weak. In the two or three plates, the price of the second-grade yarn rose by 3 or 4 yuan, and each month rose by 4, 5, and 7 qian. The transaction totaled 36,200 bales, and Gongtai sold 2,550 bales, Taixing 2,300 bales, Xincheng 2,350 bales, and Yiyu 1,600 bales. The Spot Yarn Sales Are Active and the Price Is Flat The sales of spot yarn are more active. The market was flat, and the customers from Sichuan entered 1,500 bales, the mainland entered 160 bales, Shantou entered 125 bales, Guangdong entered 190 bales, Zhenjiang entered 30 bales, Tianjin entered 115 bales, and the North Gang entered 65 bales.

Cotton Market: Morning Weakness, Afternoon Strength 185

The cotton market was quite weak in the morning due to the meager upward momentum of American cotton and the weakening exchange rate, which made foreign cotton cheaper to purchase. Furthermore, large traders were selling off unusually vigorously, with some buying foreign cotton to arbitrage against domestic spot cotton, leading to a sharper decline. Market sentiment was very poor. In the afternoon, Grade 3 cotton suddenly rose by one yuan, also because of news that the New York and Liverpool areas of the United States would reduce new cotton acreage next year. This greatly stimulated market sentiment, buyers became active, and the market rose by 30 copper cash. However, domestic and foreign factories are currently not buying cotton, and the future is still seen as mostly bearish. Nevertheless, local Shanghai cotton merchants are inclined to go long, due to the impact of water damage on this year's harvest.

Hankow Cotton: Near-term Decline, Long-term Rise. The Hankow cotton market opened weak in the morning, with American cotton showing a slight increase but with weak market sentiment and a lack of buyers. Prices for all months fell by 20-30 copper cash. In the afternoon, due to positive news, prices rose by 20-35 copper cash. Total transactions amounted to 97,900 bales. Sales included 3,500 bales from Rui Da, 2,800 bales from Tian Long, 2,400 bales from Yu Chang, 2,000 bales from Xin Cheng, 2,500 bales from Heng Da, and 500 bales from Da Ji. Purchases included 3,000 bales from Mei Ji, 4,700 bales from Yuan Da, 2,500 bales from Da Chang, and 2,900 bales from Shen Chang. The closing prices for Hankow cotton are recorded below:

Spot Cotton: High Prices, No Transactions. Inquiries for spot cotton have disappeared because prices are too high. Foreign Cotton Yarn: Mostly Rises, Few Declines 186

American cotton continued its upward trend. Yesterday, American cotton was initially firm due to good news from Liverpool, but later weakened due to weakness on Wall Street and mass selling. Indian cotton initially rose with American cotton but then weakened due to profit-taking. Finally, it firmed again due to good news from Liverpool. News on US Cotton Acreage Restriction Plan 187

A New Orleans telegram dated the 21st stated that Governor Long's plan to prohibit cotton planting has been approved by the New Orleans Cotton Conference. At the same time, his proposal to have the Department of Agriculture purchase 8 million bales at higher prices, based on the opinions of farmers, was also adopted. Previously, on the 17th, Governor Long had invited the governors and senators of the cotton-planting states to hold a meeting on the 21st to discuss the constitutionality of prohibiting cotton planting in each state next year.

US Cotton Frequently Hits New Lows Last Week 188

New Crop Growing Smoothly Compared to Previous Years

Long Traders Have No Way to Intervene

A telegram from New York dated the 21st reported on the cotton market during the week: The cotton market continued to decline last week because the growth of the new crop this month has been better than the previous average. Based on this yield, the market price is expected to see new lows. Currently, it is speculated that the increase in new crop movement and the increase in the government's next production estimate have caused long traders to liquidate. Even new buyers are reselling. Price declines have prompted some buying from industry insiders and short covering, but rallies are quickly halted. Market sentiment is completely bearish, with little hope for improvement. The strong bearish sentiment is quite rare, and long traders have practically no way to intervene. Weekend statistics are appended below (in thousands of bales):

Rice Market in River Towns Weakens Daily 189

Yesterday, the supply from various sources in the southern market was still thin, and river stocks were abundant. Due to the hot weather, retail sales in towns and villages were slow, and stores did not keep large inventories. The price of thick japonica rice suddenly decreased by 20-30 copper cash. The arrival of thin indica rice was somewhat sluggish. Local sales remained slow, and the local market remained sluggish, causing prices to fall again by a few copper cash. Although there wasn't a large amount of high-quality Xu Lu and Yang Jian rice, only the fresh varieties were selling. The market remained flat, and small sales of converted Yin Yuan were steady.

Goods from Zhabei Road were not moving well, and Jiangsu and Changzhou white japonica rice was quite sluggish, with prices falling by 200 copper cash. Early and late season rice was difficult to move, and prices had not returned to lower levels after several days of waiting. Buying interest was stronger than the previous day, and the situation seemed set. There was little demand for foreign Lu Jian rice, and sales of converted Yin Yuan were slow. Sales of Kunshan rice and Liyang-Yixing rice were extremely weak, with prices decreasing by 200-300 copper cash. Approximately 2,000 dan of river town rice arrived.

Flour Market Turns Firm in the Afternoon 190

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, prices for all months were flat and weak due to a slight increase in the quoted price of foreign wheat. This month briefly broke through the one copper cash mark, but Tianjin merchants became active and prices stabilized. By the afternoon, real demand buyers were actively purchasing due to the low market value, with Tianjin merchants being the most active. Outside speculation that the US wheat loan to China might be difficult to achieve due to the harsh conditions recorded in the telegrams of the day boosted market sentiment, and buying interest became active again. Observation of the situation suggests that prices may fluctuate for a few days. As a result, this month improved by one copper cash compared to the previous day, September/October improved by 0.05 copper cash, November/December improved by one copper cash, and January improved by 1.25 copper cash.

Wheat Milling Active, Wheat Futures Show Common Color 191

Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed a flat and stable trend for all months after opening in the morning and afternoon. For this month, as delivery is imminent, the short sellers' delivery reserves are reportedly around 200 truckloads. On the long side, large traders have already sold off, and most of the current positions are held by inland merchants. Their ability to take delivery seems limited. Mills have ample foreign wheat and will not take delivery, so market sentiment is quite flat. Distant months are slightly better due to the difficulty in securing the US wheat loan. As a result, this month was down 0.01 copper cash compared to the previous day, September/October were down 0.01 copper cash, November was down 0.02 copper cash, December was down 0.01 copper cash, and January was down 0.02 copper cash. Spot wheat milling was good, and the market also turned brisk. More than 5,000 bags were traded throughout the day. Six-Hop wheat was offered at 3.79 to 3.76 taels, Wuxi wheat at 3.77 taels, and Pudong Anting wheat at 3.7 taels. Zhitang Penglai wheat was offered at 3.75-3.76 taels, and Yangzhou Six-Hop, Jiangbei Zhenjiang, etc. wheat was offered at 3.74-3.75 taels.

North-South Goods: Lanxi Jujubes Fall Again and Again 192

Lanxi jujubes, which had previously fallen to just over 30 taels due to large arrivals, are now weakening due to sluggish sales. Yesterday, the bare selling price had reached 24 taels, more than 10 taels lower than the highest price. The market seems temporarily stable, but in the long term, if supplies continue to arrive in large quantities, prices could fall to 20 taels.

Silk and Tea: European and American Silk Sales Increase 193

Overseas raw silk markets saw gradual increases in sales from raw silk factories. As Japanese silk prices were low, Shanghai Chinese silk firms found local prices to be too high and telegrams were sparse. Yesterday, only China Trading imported 10 bales of Shanghai white factory silk, and Jardine and others imported 40 bales of gray factory silk. Prices remained firm.

Wuyuan Green Tea: Large American Orders Continue 194

Yesterday, Wuyuan natural, pure grade green tea continued to be popular with American firms. Jardine, Jinlong, and other firms, as well as the China Tea Company, were all interested, and transactions were quite brisk. Prices were similar to before. Firms such as Yongxing, Tianxiang, Jinlong, and Tongfu were all interested in local Zhen Mei tea, but they were offering slightly lower prices than before. However, as Chinese merchants had low inventories and exhausted sources, they were firm in their position and unwilling to sell at lower prices. In addition, there were scattered transactions in needle tea, aged tea, and other items, and the market was unusually stable.

Oil Market: Hankou White Tung Oil After Flooding 195

Lack of Arrivals...Transactions Completely Quiet

Local Villages...Sales Market Slightly Active

After the flooding in Hankou, the streets became waterways, business was suspended, and loading was difficult. There were no transactions in either the domestic or foreign markets. It was reported that foreign firms had sold at 23 taels Shanghai currency per pound before the flooding, but no bids have been made since. Domestic sales have become even quieter due to the continued rise in water levels. The local villages have not been greatly affected by the flooding and have been paying more attention to lacquer work due to the hot weather and lack of work in the fields, so the market in nearby villages has been slightly active. The road is still waiting. However, Hankou tung oil cannot arrive in Shanghai for the time being due to the inconvenience of loading. It will have to wait for the water to recede before loading can be resumed. As a result, Shanghai firms are very short of Hankou tung oil. Although sales are not brisk, they are already stretched thin.

Piece Goods: Domestically Produced Woolens Sell Well 196

Domestically produced woolens have been selling quite well lately. As early autumn has arrived, buyers are actively purchasing wide and narrow stripes and solid-color camel wool, resulting in the most transactions. Shengda Dragon and Phoenix, Xinda Camel Brand, Weilun Tiger, Weiyi Double Deer, and Hongfa Tianxiang brands are all selling at 1.65 taels per yard. Five-color stripes are priced at 2.175 taels. All prices are for delivery in Shanghai. For export to other ports, an additional 0.01 tael per yard is required. Zhanghua small cap flannel sells for 3.5 to 4.25 taels. Cap makers are actively selecting and ordering Ningbo Jiangshan horsehair interlining at 1.25 yuan per ruler, and tailors are buying 9-inch material at 0.3 yuan per yard.

Metals: Tinplate Purchased by Cigarette Factories 197

Yesterday, cigarette factories purchased tinplate, causing the market to suddenly become lively. Although prices did not rise, market sentiment was very good. The total number of boxes offered throughout the city was over 690, with 90-pound English goods priced at 14 taels and 100-pound goods at 15 taels. 90-pound American goods were priced at 16.25 taels, and 100-pound goods at 17 taels. It was reported that the majority of the goods offered were 200-pound sizes, priced at 30 taels.
